The unprecedented situation caused us to stay home, and sometimes in small spaces for some of us. We are forced to have limited interactions with one another. I found, only after a week, that it was not sitting well with many of my  friends. Many of them became depressed and started developing anxiety. I am not saying it didn\u2019t affect me, but I felt at ease with it in a way. Those who really know me wouldn\u2019t be surprised because I LOVE being home. \\nThe film \u201cTOGETHER\u201d has a purpose to bring smiles, positivity, and hope. This is a great way to overcome negative emotions, to stay positive, and to grow as well.\\nThere's a certain feeling of pride that goes with keeping yourself busy.
